Lives and Works of Three Hanafi Authorities
Biographical entries on three Hanafi scholars and their major works

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the three scholars and their major works and state the significance of each for Hanafi fatwa practice.

Core Idea
Ibn Nujaym, Mulla Miskin, and al-Zahidi authored foundational texts that every Hanafi mufti must know.

This lesson introduces three influential Hanafi scholars from different centuries: Ibn Nujaym (10th c.), Mulla Miskin (10th c.), and al-Zahidi (7th c.). Their works—al-Bahr al-Raiq, al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir, and commentaries on Kanz al-Daqa'iq—are cornerstones of Hanafi fiqh and fatwa methodology. Understanding who they are and what they wrote helps you navigate the Hanafi tradition with confidence.

Guided Path
1
Identify each scholar and his era
Read the Arabic passage to extract the full name, death date (in Hijri), and region of each scholar: Ibn Nujaym (d. 950), Mulla Miskin (d. 954), and al-Zahidi (d. 5658? likely 658).
Death dates help assess the reliability and temporal relevance of their works.
2
List the major works of each scholar
For Ibn Nujaym, note his works: al-Bahr al-Raiq (commentary on Kanz al-Daqa'iq), Fatawa Zayniyya, Majmu'at Rasa'il Zayniyya, and al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir. For Mulla Miskin: his commentary on Kanz. For al-Zahidi: no works explicitly named but noted as a great jurist.
These works are frequently cited in later fatwa collections.
3
Recognize the special features of these works
Note that al-Bahr al-Raiq was left incomplete by Ibn Nujaym and completed by al-Turi. Al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir covers seven arts including hiyal (legal stratagems). Mulla Miskin's commentary is known as Sharh Mulla Miskin.
Knowing these details prevents misattribution when consulting the texts.
4
Connect the scholars to fatwa practice
These authors are part of the chain of authority in the Hanafi school. Their works are used by later muftis like Ibn Abidin (who quotes from them in Rasm al-Mufti). Recognizing their names helps you evaluate the weight of a ruling.
In fatwa, citing a recognized authority strengthens your response.

Ibn Nujaym, Allama Zayn al-Din ibn Ibrahim al-Misri (d. 950), a famous Hanafi jurist of the 10th century, known as Ibn Nujaym al-Misri and Zayn ibn Nujaym. His works include: (1) Sharh al-Bahr al-Raiq, a commentary on Kanz al-Daqa'iq, in eight volumes, printed. He wrote up to the book of Ijarah, chapter of invalid ijarah; this chapter was not completed before his death; the completion was written by Shaykh Muhammad ibn Husayn al-Turi al-Qadiri (d. after 1138). The eighth volume is the completion. (2) Fatawa Zayniyya. (3) Majmu'at Rasa'il Zayniyya (collection of 41 treatises). (4) al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir, comprising seven arts: (1) General Qawaid, (2) General Dawabit, (3) Art of Combining and Differentiating, (4) Puzzles (fiqh riddles), (5) Legal Stratagems, (6) Similarities and Analogies, and (7) Anecdotes. The book is named after the part. Several commentaries have been written on it. al-Ramli wrote a gloss. Three famous commentaries are: (1) al-Tahqiq al-Bahir Sharh al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Allama Taj al-Din Muhammad Hibbatallah ibn Muhammad Ba'li al-Taji al-Dimashqi (d. 1224), manuscript in three volumes; Allama Shami quotes from it in Rasm al-Mufti. (2) Ghumuz 'Uyun al-Basa'ir fi Sharh al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Allama Ahmad ibn Muhammad Abu al-Abbas Shihab al-Din al-Hamawi al-Misri (d. 1098), known as 'Sharh Hamawi'; printed in four volumes and widely used. al-Hamawi was prolific; many of his books are mentioned in A'lam, volume 2, p. 239. (3) 'Umdat Dhawi al-Basa'ir li-Hall Muhimmat al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by Allama Birri Ibrahim ibn Husayn al-Hanafi, Mufti of Makka (d. 1099?); manuscript in Istanbul; Allama Shami frequently quotes from it in Rasm al-Mufti. -32 Mulla Miskin Mu'in al-Din al-Harawi (d. 954), wrote a commentary on Kanz, printed as Sharh Mulla Miskin. By merging the nun of 'Munda' into lam it is also said 'Mulla'. This Turkish word is synonymous with 'Allama.' He was among the great imams, leaders of the nuqaba', a perfect scholar, having extensive knowledge in ikhtilaf and madhhab, and skill in discourse and debate (Fawa'id Bahiyya p. 88). This passage continues the biographical appendix of Rasm al-Mufti, introducing three Hanafi scholars: Ibn Nujaym, Mulla Miskin, and al-Zahidi. For each, it lists major works and provides contextual details, such as the unfinished state of al-Bahr al-Raiq and the commentaries on al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir. The inclusion of these scholars indicates the authorities that later Hanafi fatwa literature draws upon. The mention of al-Zahidi's praise highlights his stature. These notes help students recognize the key reference works and their authors in the Hanafi tradition.

Key Terms
البحر الرائق (al-Bahr al-Raiq): Ibn Nujaym's commentary on Kanz al-Daqa'iq, meaning 'The Clear Sea'; a major Hanafi fiqh reference.
الاشباه والنظائر (al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir): Ibn Nujaym's work on legal maxims and analogous cases, covering seven disciplines including qawaid, dawabit, and hiyal.
ملا مسکین (Mulla Miskin): Title of Mu'in al-Din al-Harawi, meaning 'Mulla Miskin', derived from Turkish 'Munda' with nun merged into lam.
حیل (hiyal): Legal stratagems; permissible ways to achieve a lawful outcome without violating the Shari'ah.

Evaluating Hanafi Source Reliability for Fatwa
Biographical notes with reliability assessments

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify reliable and unreliable Hanafi sources based on author's creed and transmission strength, and apply this to evaluate a given work.

Core Idea
Not every book by a Hanafi scholar is reliable; the author's creed and transmission chain determine its authority for fatwa.

In Hanafi fatwa, not all books are created equal. Some works, despite being written by Hanafi jurists, contain weak transmissions or doctrinal issues that make them unreliable. This lesson uses the example of 'Qunyah' and other works to teach you how to critically assess a source before relying on it for fatwa.

Guided Path
1
Identify the scholar and his work
From the biographical note, name the scholar and the specific book being evaluated. For example, 'Allamah Zahidi and his book Qunyah.
2
Check the author's creed
Determine if the author was a Sunni or held deviant beliefs (e.g., Mu'tazili). The passage indicates Zahidi was Mu'tazili.
Even if the author is a Hanafi in fiqh, his creed may affect the reliability of his narrations.
3
Assess transmission strength
Look for comments on the transmission chain. Qunyah is described as having weak transmissions (riwayat da'ifah).
Weak transmission can arise from unreliable narrators or lack of verification.
4
Determine reliability
If the author is non-Sunni or transmissions are weak, the book is unreliable unless corroborated by other reliable sources.
The passage states: 'until his statements are verified by other books, all his books are unreliable.'
5
Apply to a new case
Given a different Hanafi work from a later scholar, apply the same criteria to decide if it can be used in fatwa.
For instance, 'Umar ibn Nujaym's al-Nibr al-Fa'iq is incomplete but by a reliable author; it may be used with caution.

Source Text

علامہ شامی نے رسم المفتی میں اس سے عبارتیں نقل کی ہیں ۔ (۲) غمز عيون البصائر فی شرح الاشباه والنظائر از علامہ احمد بن محمد ابو العباس شہاب راز علامه احمدبن محمد ابو الجبال شباب الدین حموی مصری رحمہ اللہ (متوفی ۱۰۹۸) یہ شرح حموی“ سے بھی معروف ہے۔ چار جلدوں میں مطبوعہ اور متداول ہے۔ حموی کثیر التصانیف ہیں۔ اعلام ج اص ۲۳۹ میں ان کی بہت سی کتابوں کا تذکرہ ہے۔ (۳) عمدة ذوى البصائر لحل مہمات الاشباه والنظائر از علامہ بیری ابراہیم بن حسین حنفی مفتی مکہ مکرمہ (۱۳۳۱ ایف ۱۰۹۹ھ ) استنبول میں اس کا مخطوطہ ہے۔ علامہ شامی رسم المفتی میں اس سے بکثرت نقل کرتے ہیں۔ ۳۲- منلا مسکین معین الدین ہروی رحمہ اللہ (متوفی ۹۵۴ ھ ) آپ نے کنزر کی شرح لکھی ہے جو شرح منلا مسکین کے نام سے مطبوعہ ہے۔ منڈا کے نون کا لام میں ادغام کر کے ملا بھی کہتے ہیں۔ یہ ترکی لفظ ہے جو علامہ کا مترادف ہے۔ علامہ زاہدی، مختار بن محمود ابو الرجاء نجم الدین رحمہ اللہ (متوفی ۵۶۵۸ ) ساتویں صدی کے مشہور حنفی فقیہ ہیں۔ کان من کبار الائمۃہ داعیان النقباء عالماً كاملاً له اليد الباسطة في الخلاف والمذهب والباع الطويل في الكلام والمناظرة ( فوائد ببیہ ص ۸۸ ) مگر علامہ ابن وہبان کے خیال میں معتزلی عقیدہ کے تھے صرف فروع میں حنفی تھے۔ اس لیے جب تک دوسری کتابوں سے ان کی باتوں کی مطابقت نہ ہو جائے ان کی سب کتابیں غیر معتبر ہیں۔ ان کی کتابیں رطب و یابس کا مجموعہ بھی میں (فوائد بیبیہ ) مولی برکلی (۳۷) کہتے ہیں کہ تمام غیر معتبر کتابوں میں سر فہرست قنیہ ہے۔ اگر چہ بعض علماء نے اپنی کتابوں میں قنیہ سے نقل کیا ہے مگر وہ علماء کے نزدیک ضعیف روایتوں میں مشہور ہے اور اس کا مصنف معتزلی ہے ( کشف الظنون ج ۲ ص ۱۳۵۷) آپ کی تصانیف یہ ہیں (۱) قنیہ المنیتہ تقسیم الغنیہ (صرف قنیہ سے مشہور ہے) مطبوعہ ہے اور مدینہ الفقہاء کا خلاصہ ہے جو آپ کے استاذ علامہ بدیع بن منصور عراقی کی تصنیف ہے (۲) قدوری کی شرح مجتبی جو ہنوز مخطوطہ ہے۔ (۳) زاد الائمہ وغیرہ۔ ۳۴- علامہ عمر بن ابراہیم سراج الدین ابن نجیم مصری رحمہ اللہ (متوفی شاھ ) مشہور حنفی فقیہ اور ابن نجیم (۳۱) صاحب بحر کے چھوٹے بھائی ہیں۔ عمر بن نجیم سے مشہور ہیں آپ نے کنز الدقائق کی شرح النبر الفائق لکھی ہے جو ہنوز مخطوطہ ہے۔ یہ شرح مکمل نہیں ہے ۔ کتاب القضاء فضل الحبس تک ہے۔ پھر کوئی مانع پیش آگیا جس کی وجہ سے تعمیل نہ کر سکے ( کشف الظنون ج ۲ ص ۱۵۱۷) آپ کی ایک کتاب اجابته السائل بھی ہے جس میں طرطوی (۵۰) کی انفع الوسائل کی تلخیص کی ہے یہ بھی مخطوطہ ہے۔ ۳۵ - علامہ عینی بدر الدین محمود بن احمد رحمہ اللہ (۷۶ ھ فر ۵۸۵۵ ) مشہور حنفی فقیہ اور بہت بڑے محدث اور مؤرخ ہیں۔ آپ کی بخاری شریف کی بے مثال شرح عمدۃ القاری اور ہدایہ کی شرح البنا یہ معروف مطبوعہ کتابیں ہیں آپ نے کنز کی بھی شرح لکھی ہے جس کا نام رمز الحقائق ہے ۔ مگر یہ تینوں کتابیں آپ کے نام سے بھی معروف ہیں ۔ اول عینی شرح بخاری ثانی مینی شرح ہدایہ ثالث عینی شرح کنز کہلاتی ہے۔ آپ کثیر التصانیف نہیں۔ -۳۶- شیخ صالح بن ابراہیم جینینی حنفی رحمہ اللہ ( ۹: اه ف اے لاھ ) مشہور حنفی عالم ہیں ۔ جینین فلسطین میں ایک مقام ہے۔ بڑے محدث بھی ہیں اور بعلی (۳۱) کے استاذ ہیں۔ ۳۷ - علامہ محی الدین محمد بن پیر علی برکلی (برکوی) رومی رحمہ اللہ ( ۹۲۹ اف ۹۸ ھ ) مشہور نحوی صرفی حنفی فقیہ اور محدث ہیں آپ کی فقہی تصنیفات یہ ہیں (۱) شرح وقایہ کا حاشیہ (۲) ذخیرة المحتالين والنساء في تعريف الاطهار والدماء (۳) رسالة في حرمة الغنی (۴) السیف الصارم على
The commentary of the sea al-rai'q (clear sea) is printed in eight volumes. Up to the book of ijarah, chapter of invalid ijarah, it is from your pen. This chapter was not completed when the appointed time arrived; the completion was written by Shaykh Muhammad bin Husayn Turi Qadiri (died after 1138 AH). The eighth volume is the completion. (2) Fatawa Zayniyya (3) Majmu'ah Rasa'il Zayniyya (a collection of 41 treatises) (4) al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir (comprising seven arts: (1) general maxims, (2) general principles, (3) art of combining and differentiating, (4) riddles (fiqh puzzles), (5) stratagems (fiqh measures), (6) similarities and differences, and (7) anecdotes). The book is named 'Juz' and multiple commentaries have been written on it. Ramli (28) wrote a gloss. Its known commentaries are three as follows: (1) al-Tahqiq al-Bahir Sharh al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by 'Allamah Taj al-Din Muhammad Hibbatullah bin Muhammad Ba'li Taji, Dimashqi (died 115 AH? d. 1224 AH). Its manuscript exists in three volumes. 'Allamah Shami quoted passages from it in Rasm al-Mufti. (2) Ghumz 'Uyun al-Basa'ir fi Sharh al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by 'Allamah Ahmad bin Muhammad Abu al-'Abbas Shihab Raz? 'Allamah Ahmad bin Muhammad Abu al-Jibal Shabab al-Din Hamawi Misri (died 1098). This commentary is also known as 'Hamawi'. It is printed and in circulation in four volumes. Hamawi is prolific in works. In A'lam, vol. 3, p. 239, many of his books are mentioned. (3) 'Umdat Dhuwi al-Basa'ir li Hall Muhimmat al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir by 'Allamah Biri Ibrahim bin Husayn Hanafi, Mufti of Makkah (1331 F? d. 1099 AH). Its manuscript is in Istanbul. 'Allamah Shami quotes from it extensively in Rasm al-Mufti. 32- Mulla Miskin Mu'in al-Din Harawi (d. 954 AH). He wrote a commentary on Kanz, which is printed as 'Sharh Mulla Miskin'. By merging the nun of 'munda' into the lam, it is also called 'mulla'. This is a Turkish word synonymous with 'allamah'. 33- 'Allamah Zahidi, Mukhtar bin Mahmud Abu al-Raja' Najm al-Din (d. 5658? 7th century). He is a famous Hanafi jurist of the 7th century. He was among the great imams, leaders, learned and perfect, having a broad command in divergence and school, and a long reach in discourse and debate (Fawa'id Bahiyya p. 88). However, according to 'Allamah Ibn Wahban, he held Mu'tazili creed and was Hanafi only in subsidiary matters. Therefore, until his statements are verified by other books, all his books are unreliable. His books are a collection of wet and dry (i.e., mixed). In Fawa'id Bahiyya, Mawla Barkali (37) says that foremost among all unreliable books is Qunyah. Although some scholars have quoted from Qunyah in their books, it is known among scholars for weak transmissions and its author is a Mu'tazili (Kashf al-Zunun vol. 2 p. 1357). His works are: (1) Qunyah al-Munyah li Takmish al-Ghaniyyah (famous simply as Qunyah), printed, and it is a summary of Madinat al-Fuqaha' which is a work of his teacher 'Allamah Badi' bin Mansur 'Iraqi. (2) Commentary on Quduri's Mujtaba, still manuscript. (3) Zad al-A'imma etc. 34- 'Allamah 'Umar bin Ibrahim Siraj al-Din Ibn Nujaym Misri (d. ...?), famous Hanafi jurist and younger brother of Ibn Nujaym (31), author of Bahr. He is known as 'Umar bin Nujaym. He wrote a commentary on Kanz al-Daqa'iq called al-Nibr al-Fa'iq, still manuscript. This commentary is incomplete; it goes up to the book of Qada' and chapter of Fadl al-Habs. Then some obstacle prevented completion (Kashf al-Zunun vol. 2 p. 1517). He also has a book Ijabatuhu al-Sa'il in which he summarized Tartawi's (50) Anfa' al-Wasa'il; this is also manuscript. 35- 'Allamah 'Ayni Badr al-Din Mahmud bin Ahmad (d. 76? 855?). He is a famous Hanafi jurist, a great muhaddith and historian. His unparalleled commentary on Sahih al-Bukhari, 'Umdat al-Qari, and his commentary on al-Hidayah, al-Binayah, are well-known printed books. He also wrote a commentary on Kanz named Ramz al-Haqa'iq. These three books are also known by his name: first is 'Ayni's commentary on Bukhari, second is 'Ayni's commentary on Hidayah, third is 'Ayni's commentary on Kanz. He is not prolific. 36- Shaykh Salih bin Ibrahim Jayshini Hanafi (d. ...?). He is a famous Hanafi scholar. Jayshin is a place in Palestine. He is also a great muhaddith and teacher of Ba'li (31). 37- 'Allamah Muhyi al-Din Muhammad bin Pir 'Ali Barkali (Barkawi) Rumi (d. 929? 98?). He is a famous grammarian, lexicologist, Hanafi jurist, and muhaddith. His fiqh works are: (1) Gloss on Sharh Wiqayah, (2) Dhakhirat al-Muhtalin wa al-Nisa' fi Ta'rif al-Atthar wa al-Dima', (3) Risalah fi Hurmat al-Ghina', (4) al-Sayf al-Sarim 'ala...
Source pages p. 153

Commentary
This passage is a continuation of the section on Sharh Rasm al-Mufti, which provides biographical and bibliographic notes on Hanafi scholars and their works. The text begins with the author's own works and their commentaries, then moves to a numbered list of scholars from number 32 onward. The first part describes a commentary on al-Ashbah wa al-Naza'ir and lists three well-known commentaries of that book. Then it presents brief biographies of several Hanafi figures: Mulla Miskin, known for his commentary on Kanz; 'Allamah Zahidi, whom the author warns is unreliable due to Mu'tazili beliefs, especially his book Qunyah; 'Umar bin Nujaym, who wrote an incomplete commentary on Kanz; 'Allamah 'Ayni, a famous muhaddith and historian with commentaries on Bukhari, Hidayah, and Kanz; Shaykh Salih bin Ibrahim al-Jayshini, a muhaddith and teacher; and lastly 'Allamah Barkali (Barkawi), a grammarian and jurist. The entry for Barkali is cut off mid-sentence. The author includes critical evaluations, particularly the warning about relying on Zahidi's works unless corroborated. This passage serves as a reference for users of Rasm al-Mufti to identify authoritative sources and avoid weak ones.

Key Terms
منلا مسکین (Mulla Miskin): Title of a scholar named Mu'in al-Din Harawi, known for his commentary on Kanz al-Daqa'iq.
علامہ زاہدی ('Allamah Zahidi): Mukhtar bin Mahmud Abu al-Raja' Najm al-Din, a 7th-century Hanafi jurist but criticized for Mu'tazili beliefs.
قنیہ (Qunyah): A book by 'Allamah Zahidi, a summary of Madinat al-Fuqaha'.
ابن نجیم (Ibn Nujaym): Common surname of two Hanafi scholars: Zayn al-Din (author of Bahr) and his younger brother 'Umar (author of al-Nibr al-Fa'iq).
علامہ عینی ('Allamah 'Ayni): Badr al-Din Mahmud bin Ahmad, famous Hanafi jurist, muhaddith, historian, author of 'Umdat al-Qari and al-Binayah.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
Why is the book 'Qunyah' considered unreliable according to the passage?
A) It contains grammatical errors.
B) Its author was a Mu'tazili and its transmissions are weak.
C) It is only a summary of another book.
D) It was written by a non-Hanafi.

Key Takeaway
The reliability of a Hanafi source depends on the author's creed and transmission strength; weak sources like Qunyah require corroboration.

Life of the Author
intermediate
8 min
Assessing Hanafi Fiqh Authorities: Reliability of Authors
Biographical notices with a warning about unreliable books

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the criterion for unreliability of Hanafi books and list the key works of the mentioned scholars, applying the principle to fatwa practice.

Core Idea
A Hanafi book's reliability depends on the doctrinal soundness of its author.

This passage from a Rasm al-Mufti work warns muftis not to rely blindly on any book labeled Hanafi. It highlights that doctrinal deviation (like Mu'tazilism) renders a work suspect. Then it surveys six notable Hanafi scholars, listing their contributions so that muftis can recognize authoritative sources. Understanding this hierarchy is essential for issuing sound fatwas.

Guided Path
1
Identify the reliability criterion
Find the sentence that states when a Hanafi book is unreliable. The passage says any book whose author was Mu'tazili is unreliable unless corroborated.
2
Spot the prime example
Which book is singled out as the most unreliable? Qunyah is mentioned as the foremost.
Note that some scholars quote from it, but it is known for weak narrations.
3
Parse each biography
For scholars 34-39, list their name, death date (if given), major works, and any special status (e.g., ijtihad for Ibn al-Humam).
Focus on which works are considered authoritative (e.g., Fath al-Qadir).
4
Connect to fatwa practice
Determine which of these works would be acceptable for deriving fatwa based on the passage's criteria (sound creed and verifiable chain).
E.g., Fath al-Qadir is used, Qunyah is not.
5
Formulate the principle
Summarize the rule for muftis: only use works from authors who are Sunni in creed and whose works are verified by other reliable sources.
This is a recurring theme in Rasm al-Mufti literature.

۳۵ - علامہ عینی بدر الدین محمود بن احمد رحمہ اللہ (۷۶ ھ فر ۵۸۵۵ ) مشہور حنفی فقیہ اور بہت بڑے محدث اور مؤرخ ہیں۔ آپ کی بخاری شریف کی بے مثال شرح عمدۃ القاری اور ہدایہ کی شرح البنا یہ معروف مطبوعہ کتابیں ہیں آپ نے کنز کی بھی شرح لکھی ہے جس کا نام رمز الحقائق ہے ۔ مگر یہ تینوں کتابیں آپ کے نام سے بھی معروف ہیں ۔ اول عینی شرح بخاری ثانی مینی شرح ہدایہ ثالث عینی شرح کنز کہلاتی ہے۔ آپ کثیر التصانیف نہیں۔ -۳۶- شیخ صالح بن ابراہیم جینینی حنفی رحمہ اللہ ( ۹: اه ف اے لاھ ) مشہور حنفی عالم ہیں ۔ جینین فلسطین میں ایک مقام ہے۔ بڑے محدث بھی ہیں اور بعلی (۳۱) کے استاذ ہیں۔ ۳۷ - علامہ محی الدین محمد بن پیر علی برکلی (برکوی) رومی رحمہ اللہ ( ۹۲۹ اف ۹۸ ھ ) مشہور نحوی صرفی حنفی فقیہ اور محدث ہیں آپ کی فقہی تصنیفات یہ ہیں (۱) شرح وقایہ کا حاشیہ (۲) ذخیرة المحتالين والنساء في تعريف الاطهار والدماء (۳) رسالة في حرمة الغنی (۴) السیف الصارم على عدم جواز وقف المعقول والدراہم (باقی کتابوں کے نام ہدیہ العارفین ج ۲ ص ۲۵۲ اور اعدام ج 4 ص ۶۱ میں دیکھیں ۔ )
* ٠٣, السراج الوہاج الموضح لكل طالب و محتاج آٹھ جلدوں میں قدوری کی شرح ہے اور مخطوطہ ہے۔ مصنف علامہ حداد (لوہار ) ابو بکر بن علی الحداد الزبیدی رحمہ اللہ (متوفی ۸۰۰ ) میں پھر آپ نے اس کی دو جلدوں میں تلخیص کی ہے جس کا نام الجوہرۃ النیر ہ ہے جو مطبوعہ ہے۔ آپ کا تعلق یمن کے علاقہ عبادیہ سے تھا وفات یمن کے مشہور قصبہ زبید میں ہوئی ہے۔ علامہ خدادی اور علامہ الحداد سے آپ مشہور ہیں۔ آپ کے سوانح نگاروں نے آپ کے متعلق لکھا ہے کہ لہ فی مذہب ابی حنیفہ مصنفات جلیلہ لم يصنف احد من العماء الجحفية باليمن مثلبها کثرة وافادة ( اعلام ج ۲ ص ۱۷)
-۳۹- علامه ابن الہمام ) ہمام بہادر یخی سردار کمال الدین محمد بن عبد الواحد سیواسی اسکندری رحمہ اللہ ( 2900 ھ ف الھ ) نوین صدی کے مشہور حنفی امام مذاہب اربعہ کے اصولوں کے ماہر علم کلام کے شناور اور علوم عقلیہ کے جامع تھے۔ سیواس آبائی وطن ہے جو تر کیا میں ہے ولادت اسکندریہ میں اور وفات قاہرہ میں ہوئی ہے علامہ شامی نے لکھا ہے کہ فقہ میں آپ کو اجتہاد کا درجہ حاصل تھا ۔ (شامی ج ۲ ص ۳۸۸) آپ کی سب کتابیں مطبوعہ ہیں اور وہ یہ ہیں (۱) فتح القدير للحاجز الفقير (محتاج و عاجز بندے پر رب قدیر کی کشائش ) ہدایہ کی معروف شرح ہے مگر مکمل نہیں کر سکے تھے کہ وقت موعود آ پہنچانہ کتاب الوکالہ شروع کی تھی پر علامہ شمس الدین احمد بن قو در معروف به قاضی زاده (متوفی ۹۸۸ھ) نے جھیل کی۔ علامہ ابن الہمام نے راج الدین عمر بن علی کمتانی (متوفی ۱۲۹ھ) سے انیس سال ہدایہ تحقیق واتقان کے ساتھ پڑھی ہے۔ پھر استاذ کے بعد خود پڑھانی شروع کی اور ساتھ ہی شرح بھی لکھنی شروع کی۔ ملاعلی قاری کا فتح القدیر پر دو جلدوں میں حاشیہ بھی ہے جو غیر مطبوعہ ہے ( کشف الظنون ج ۲ ص ۲۰۳۴) (۲) التجرير بين اصولي الشافعية والحفیة (شافعی اور حنفی اصول فقہ کے اور در میان جمع و تادیب) یہ نہایت وقتی کتاب ہے نے اس کی دوسر جھیں مطبوعہ ہیں۔ پہلی شرح تین جلدوں میں انتقریر انجیر نامی ہے جو علامہ ابن انتر جارج (متونی یو) کی ہے (۷۲) رسم ہستی میں بکثرت اس ایسے لقول ہیں دوسری شرح پچار جلدوں میں تغیر التحریر کے نام سے ہے۔ نیا ری ..
They were Mu'tazili in belief, only in branches were Hanafi. Therefore, until their statements are matched with other books, all their books are unreliable. Their books are a collection of wet and dry. Mawla Barkaly (37) says that among all unreliable books, Qunyah is at the top. Although some scholars have quoted from Qunyah in their books, but it is famous among scholars for weak narrations and its author is Mu'tazili. His works are: (1) Qunyah al-Munyah li Takmilah al-Ghunayh (famous simply as Qunyah), published, and it is a summary of Madinah al-Fuqaha', which is the work of his teacher Allamah Badi' ibn Mansur al-Iraqi. (2) Sharh al-Mujtaba of al-Quduri, still manuscript. (3) Zad al-A'immah, etc. 34- Allamah Umar ibn Ibrahim Siraj al-Din Ibn Nujaym al-Misri (d. ...) is a famous Hanafi jurist and the younger brother of Ibn Nujaym, author of al-Bahr. They are famous as Umar ibn Nujaym. He wrote al-Nabr al-Fa'iq, a commentary on Kanz al-Daqa'iq, which is still manuscript. This commentary is incomplete. It goes up to Kitab al-Qada' wa Fadl al-Habs. Then an obstacle occurred, so he could not complete it. He also has a book Ijabah al-Sa'il, which is a summary of Turtawi's Anfa' al-Wasa'il; this is also a manuscript. 35- Allamah Ayni, Badr al-Din Mahmud ibn Ahmad (d. ...) is a famous Hanafi jurist, a great hadith scholar and historian. His unparalleled commentary on Sahih al-Bukhari, 'Umdat al-Qari, and his commentary on al-Hidayah, al-Binayah, are well-known published books. He also wrote a commentary on Kanz called Ramz al-Haqa'iq. But these three books are also known by his name: the first is called Ayni's Sharh al-Bukhari, the second is Minyari's Sharh al-Hidayah, the third is Ayni's Sharh al-Kanz. He does not have many works. 36- Shaykh Salih ibn Ibrahim al-Jinini al-Hanafi (d. ...) is a famous Hanafi scholar. Jinin is a place in Palestine. He is also a great hadith scholar and the teacher of Ba'li. 37- Allamah Muhy al-Din Muhammad ibn Pir Ali Barkali (Birgivi) al-Rumi (d. ...) is a famous grammarian, morphologist, Hanafi jurist and hadith scholar. His fiqh works are: (1) Hashiya on Sharh al-Wiqayah, (2) Dhakhirat al-Muhtalin wa al-Nisa' fi Ta'rif al-At'har wa al-Dima', (3) Risalah fi Hurmat al-Ghina, (4) al-Saif al-Sarim 'ala Adam Jawaz Waqf al-Ma'qul wa al-Darahim. (See the rest in Hadiyyat al-'Arifin vol. 2 p. 252 and A'lam vol. 4 p. 61.) * 03, al-Siraj al-Wahhaj al-Muwaddah li Kulli Talib wa Muhtaj is a commentary on al-Quduri in eight volumes and is a manuscript. Its author is Allamah Haddad (blacksmith) Abu Bakr ibn Ali al-Haddad al-Zubaidi (d. 800 AH). Then he summarized it in two volumes called al-Jawharat al-Nayyirah, which is published. He belonged to the region of 'Ubaydiyyah in Yemen and died in the famous town of Zabid in Yemen. He is famous as Allamah Khadadi and Allamah Haddad. Biographers wrote about him: 'He has magnificent works in the madhhab of Abu Hanifah; no Hanafi scholar in Yemen has written such numerous and beneficial works.' (A'lam vol. 2 p. 17) 39- Allamah Ibn al-Humam (Humam Bahadur), Kamal al-Din Muhammad ibn 'Abd al-Wahid al-Siwasiti al-Iskandari (d. ...) was a famous Hanafi imam of the ninth century, master of the principles of the four schools, an expert in kalam, and a scholar of rational sciences. Siwas is his ancestral home in Turkey; he was born in Alexandria and died in Cairo. Allamah Shami wrote that he had the rank of ijtihad in fiqh. All his books are published: (1) Fath al-Qadir li al-Hajiz al-Faqir, a famous commentary on al-Hidayah, but he could not complete it; he started the section on al-Wikalah when his time came. Then Allamah Shams al-Din Ahmad ibn Qudur known as Qadi Zadah (d. 988 AH) completed it. Ibn al-Humam studied al-Hidayah with Taj al-Din 'Umar ibn Ali al-Kummani (d. 12... AH) for nineteen years with research and perfection. Then after his teacher, he began teaching and also started writing a commentary. Mulla 'Ali al-Qari also has a commentary on Fath al-Qadir in two volumes, which is unpublished. (2) al-Tahrir bayn Usul al-Shafi'iyyah wa al-Hanafiyyah, a very valuable book; its two volumes are published. The first commentary in three volumes is called al-Taqrir al-Insiraf by Allamah Ibn Amir Hajj; there are many differences in Rasm al-Mufti; the second commentary in five volumes is called Taghrir al-Tahrir. Source pages p. 154

Commentary
This passage is a continuation of biographical entries of Hanafi jurists from a work on the methodology of giving fatwa (Rasm al-Mufti). It begins with a warning about unreliable books: any book whose author held Mu'tazili beliefs is untrustworthy unless verified by other works. The book Qunyah is cited as the foremost unreliable book. Then it lists scholars 34 to 39. Each entry provides the scholar's full name, death date, key works, and sometimes teachers or students. These biographies serve to establish the authority and reliability of the scholars whose works are used in fatwa. The passage emphasizes the importance of knowing the chain of transmission and the doctrinal soundness of authors. Among the scholars mentioned are Ibn Nujaym (author of Kanz al-Daqa'iq and its commentary), Allamah Ayni (famous for his commentary on Bukhari and Hidayah), Salih al-Jinini, Birgivi (Barkali), Ibn al-Humam (author of Fath al-Qadir), and others. The commentary style is factual; no legal analysis is needed as this is purely biographical.

Key Terms
قنیہ (Qunyah): A book of Hanafi fiqh considered unreliable due to its author's Mu'tazili beliefs.
فتح القدیر (Fath al-Qadir): A commentary on al-Hidayah by Ibn al-Humam, completed by Qadi Zadah.
اجتہاد (Ijtihad): The highest level of legal reasoning, allowing a scholar to derive rulings directly from sources.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the passage, why is the book Qunyah considered unreliable?
A) It contains many grammatical errors.
B) Its author was a Mu'tazili, so its content is suspect.
C) It is too brief and lacks detail.
D) It was written by a non-Hanafi.

Key Takeaway
A mufti must rely on works whose authors are sound in doctrine (Sunni) and whose transmission is verified.

Life of the Author
beginner
6 min
Core Hanafi Scholars in the Fatwa Tradition (43-46)
Listing biographies and works of key Hanafi scholars

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the key Hanafi scholars mentioned in the passage and state their most significant works for fatwa practice.

Core Idea
Knowing the authors behind the texts is essential for a mufti to properly weigh authority.

This passage introduces several Hanafi scholars whose works form the backbone of fatwa issuance. From al-Shurunbulali's Nur al-Idah to al-Bazzazi's fatwa collection, each scholar contributed to the school's methodology. Understanding who wrote what allows a mufti to correctly cite and evaluate rulings.

Guided Path
1
List each Hanafi scholar and his work
From the passage, extract: Amir Badsah (Sharh Rasm al-Mufti), al-Tahtawi (Hashiyat al-Durr), al-Bazzazi (Fatawa Bazzaziyyah), al-Sughdi (al-Nutaf al-Hisan), Ibn Malik (Mabaariq al-Anwar), al-Shurunbulali (Nur al-Idah, Maraqi al-Falah).
Some works like Fatawa Bazzaziyyah are printed on margins of Fatawa Alamgiri.
2
Categorize each work by genre
Determine if it's a matn (e.g., Nur al-Idah), a sharh (e.g., Sharh Rasm al-Mufti), a hashiah (e.g., Hashiyat al-Durr), or a fatwa compilation (e.g., Fatawa Bazzaziyyah).
Genre determines the work's role in fatwa hierarchy: fatwa compilations are primary, commentaries are secondary.
3
Identify the scholar's madhhab affiliation
All scholars in this lesson are Hanafi. Confirm each: All of them are explicitly mentioned as Hanafi or implied by their context.
Qadi Iyad and Ibn Taymiyyah are not Hanafi and are excluded from this lesson.
4
Memorize scholar-work pairs for quick recall
Create mental links: al-Shurunbulali → Nur al-Idah (matn on ibadat); al-Bazzazi → Fatawa Bazzaziyyah (fatwa collection). Use flashcards or mnemonic devices.
This pairing is essential for efficient fatwa research.

شرح رسم الملتي
یہ علامہ محمد امین معروف به امیر بادشاہ (متوفی ۹۷۲ھ) کی ہے (۳) المسايره في العقائد المنجية في الآخرة یہ علم کلام کا متن متین ہے۔ مسایرہ کے معنی ہیں ساتھ ساتھ چلنا ۔ چونکہ اس کتاب میں امام غزالی رحمہ اللہ کے رسالہ قدسیہ کی ترتیب ملحوظ رکھی گئی ہے۔ اس لیے مسایرہ نام رکھا ہے۔ علامہ کمال الدین محمد بن محمد معروف بابن ابی شریف قدی شافعی (متوفی ۹۵ھ) نے مسایرہ کی مسامرہ کے نام سے شرح لکھی ہے جو بعض مدارس میں پڑھائی جاتی ہے۔ (۴) زاد الفقیر
مسائل فقہیہ کا مجموعہ ہے ایک سفر میں یہ رسالہ تصنیف فرمایا ہے۔
علامہ قاضی احمد بن محمد طحطاوی ( طهطاوی) رحمہ اللہ (متوفی ۱۲۳۱ھ ) مشہور حنفی فقیه اور علامہ شامی کے استاذ ہیں آپ کی دو کتابیں مطبوعہ ہیں (۱) طحطاوی حاشیہ در مختار چار ضخیم جلدوں میں ہے (۲) طحطاوی حاشیہ مراقی الفلاح آپ کا ایک رسالہ کشف الدین عن بیان المسح
علی الجوربین مخطوطہ ہے۔ صاحب بزازیه علامه کردری ابن البز از محمد بن محمد بن شہاب رحمہ اللہ (متوفی مشہور حنفی فقیہ ہیں۔ علامہ بزازی سے مشہور ہیں آپ کی دو کتابیں مطبوعہ ہیں (۱) الجامع الوجیز جس کا مشہور نام فتاوی بزاز یہ ہے فتاویٰ عالم گیری کے حاشیہ پر از جلد نمبر ۴ تا نمبر ۶ طبع ہوئی ہے ۔ (۲) مناقب کر دری یہ امام اعظم کے مناقب میں دو جلدوں میں ہے مناقب الامام الاعظم اس کا اصل نام ہے۔ قاضی ابو الفضل عیاض بن موسیٰ شخصی رحمہ اللہ ( و ۳۷۶ ه ف ۵۲۴ ) چھٹی صدی کے مشہور مالکی فقیہ اور محدث ہیں۔ آپ کثیر التصانیف ہیں۔ چند معروف کتابیں یہ ہیں (1) الشفاء بتعريف حقوق المصطفی (سیرت نبوی میں بڑی بابرکت کتاب ہے (۲) ترتیب المدارک و تقريب المسالک علمائے مالکیہ کے احوال میں ہے) (۳) مشارق الانوار ( حدیث شریف کی کتاب ہے ) (۴) الالماع الى معرفة اصول الروايه (اصول حدیث میں ہے ) اور غیر مطبوعہ کتابوں میں مسلم شریف کی شرح ہے۔ ۴۳- علامہ ابن تیمیه شیخ الاسلام ابو العباس احمد بن عبد العلیم بن عبد السلام حرانی دمشقی (و فر (۷۲ھ) ساتویں صدی کے جلیل القدر مضبلی فقیہ بڑے محدث کثیر التصانیف عالم اور مجاہد ہیں ۔ آپ کے دادا عبدالسلام بھی بڑے محدث تھے نیل الاوطار کا متن ہمشقی من احادیث
الاحکام ابن تیمیہ جد کی مشہور کتاب ہے اور ابن تیمیہ حفید کی کتابیں یہ ہیں (۱) الصارم المسلول على شاتم الرسول (۲) رفع الملام عن الائمة الاعلام (۳) التوسل والوسيله (۴) السياسة الشرعيه في اصلاح الراعي والرعيه (۵) الفرقان بين اولياء الله واولياء الشيطان (۲) فتاوى ابن تيميه ( ۷ ) منهاج السنة وغيرہ سینکڑوں کتابوں کے مصنف ہیں۔
-۳۴
علامہ سغدی، شیخ الاسلام ابو الحسن علی بن حسین بخاری رحمہ اللہ (متوفی 21 ) پانچویں صدی کے مشہور حنفی فقیہ ہیں۔ آپ کی مشہور کتاب الخف الحسان ہے۔ نتف، نتفة کی جمع ہے جس کے معنی ہیں " تھوڑا سا' کہا جاتا ہے اعطاه نتفة من الطعام: اس نے تھوڑا سا کھانا دیا افادہ نتفة من العلم : اس نے تھوڑا سا علم سکھایا اور حسان حسنہ کی جمع ہے پس الشف الحسان کا ہے: " شاندار باتوں کا مختصر سا مجموعہ" کیونکہ یہ کتاب فتاوی کا انتخاب ہے۔ اس کا زکیا کی ٹوپ کا پی میوزیم میں ہے۔ آپ نے جامع کبیر کی بھی شرح لکھی ہے۔ فتاوی قاضی خان اور فتاوی بزازیہ میں آپ کا کثرت سے تذکرہ آتا ہے آپ شمس الائمہ سرخسی رحمہ

ابن ملک علامہ عبد اللطیف بن عبد العزیز رحمہ اللہ (متوفی نے آٹھویں صدی )
کے مشہور حنفی فقیہ اور محدث ہیں آپ کی مشارق الانوار کی شرح مبارق الانوار مطبوعہ ہے نیز المنار کی شرح بھی مطبوعہ ہے اور مجمع البحرین کی شرح مخطوطہ ہے آپ کے پردادا کا نام فرشتہ تھا
۴۶
اس لیے آپ کو عربی میں ابن ملک کہتے تھے۔ علامہ حسن بن عمار شرنبلالی رحمہ اللہ (۹۹۳ ھ فون ۱۰ھ ) گیارھویں صدی کے مشہور حنفی فقیہ ہیں۔ آپ کی مشہور کتابیں یہ ہیں (۱) نور الایضاح (۲) مراقی الفلاح شرح نور الايضاح (۳) غلیہ ذوی الاحکام فی بغیة درر الحکام (دور کے حاشیہ پر طبع ہوئی ہے) (۴) منظومه ابن وہبان کی شرح (۵) التحقيقات القدسیہ ( مجموعہ رسائل شرنبلالی کل ۴۸ رسائل ہیں). حقائق المنظومہ مفتی الثقلین علامہ مسلمی رحمہ اللہ کے منظومة الخلافیات (۲۵) کی شرح ہے شارح کا نام ابوالمحامد محمود بن محمد انسنجی بخاری ( د ۲۲۷ ف اللاھ ) ہے۔ حقائق کا مخطوطہ مدینہ منورہ میں ہے ( اعلام ج نے ص ۱۸۲)
Commentary on Rasm al-Mufti: This is by Allamah Muhammad Amin known as Amir Badsah (d. 972 AH). (3) Al-Musayah fi al-Aqaid al-Munjiyah fi al-Akhirah: This is a solid text in theology. 'Musayah' means walking together. Since this book follows the arrangement of Imam Ghazali's Risalah Qudsiyyah, it was named Musayah. Allamah Kamal al-Din Muhammad ibn Muhammad known as Ibn Abi Sharif al-Qudsi al-Shafi'i (d. 95 AH) wrote a commentary on Musayah called Musamarah, which is taught in some schools. (4) Zad al-Faqir: A collection of fiqh issues, authored during a journey. Allamah Qadi Ahmad ibn Muhammad al-Tahtawi (d. 1231 AH) is a famous Hanafi faqih and teacher of Allamah Shami. Two of his books are printed: (1) Tahtawi Hashiyah on al-Durr al-Mukhtar in four thick volumes; (2) Tahtawi Hashiyah on Maraqi al-Falah. He also has a treatise Kashf al-Din an Bayan al-Mashh ala al-Jawrabayn, which is a manuscript. The author of Bazzaziyyah, Allamah Kurdi Ibn al-Bazzaz Muhammad ibn Muhammad ibn Shihab (d. ...) is a famous Hanafi faqih. He is known as Allamah Bazzazi. Two of his books are printed: (1) al-Jami al-Wajiz, famously known as Fatawa Bazzaziyyah, printed on the margin of Fatawa Alamgiri in volumes 4-6; (2) Manaqib al-Kurdi, which is two volumes on the virtues of Imam A'zam, its original name is Manaqib al-Imam al-A'zam. Qadi Abu al-Fadl Iyad ibn Musa al-Yahsubi (d. 376 AH? d. 524 AH) is a famous Maliki faqih and muhaddith of the sixth century. He has many works. Some famous books: (1) al-Shifa bi Ta'rif Huquq al-Mustafa; (2) Tartib al-Madarik wa Taqrib al-Masalik (on Maliki scholars); (3) Mashariq al-Anwar (hadith); (4) al-Ilma' ila Ma'rifat Usul al-Riwayah (usul al-hadith); and among unpublished books, a commentary on Sahih Muslim. 43- Allamah Ibn Taymiyyah, Shaykh al-Islam Abu al-Abbas Ahmad ibn Abd al-Halim ibn Abd al-Salam al-Harrani al-Dimashqi (d. 728 AH) is a venerable Hanbali faqih, great muhaddith, prolific author, scholar, and mujahid of the seventh century. His grandfather Abd al-Salam was also a great muhaddith. Nayl al-Awtar includes the text [notes] from hadith al-ahkam. The book Ibn Taymiyyah al-Jadd is famous, and the books of Ibn Taymiyyah al-Hafid are: (1) al-Sarim al-Maslul ala Shatim al-Rasul; (2) Raf al-Malam an al-Aimmah al-Islam; (3) al-Tawassul wa al-Wasilah; (4) al-Siyasah al-Shar'iyyah fi Islah al-Rai wa al-Ra'iyyah; (5) al-Furqan bayn Awliya Allah wa Awliya al-Shaytan; (6) Fatawa Ibn Taymiyyah; (7) Minhaj al-Sunnah, and hundreds of other books. 44- Allamah al-Sughdi, Shaykh al-Islam Abu al-Hasan Ali ibn Husayn al-Bukhari (d. 21? 5th century) is a famous Hanafi faqih. His famous book is al-Nutaf al-Hisan. 'Nutaf' is the plural of 'nutfah', meaning 'a little bit'. It is said a'tahu nutfatan min al-ta'am: he gave a little food; afadahu nutfatan min al-ilm: he taught a little knowledge. 'Hisan' is plural of 'hasanah'. So al-Nutaf al-Hisan means 'a brief collection of splendid points' because this book is a selection of fatawa. A manuscript exists in the [؟] museum. He also wrote a commentary on al-Jami al-Kabir. He is frequently mentioned in Fatawa Qadikhan and Fatawa al-Bazzaziyyah. He was a student of Shams al-Aimmah al-Sarakhsi and a qadi of Bukhara. 45- Ibn Malik, Allamah Abd al-Latif ibn Abd al-Aziz (d. 8th century) is a famous Hanafi faqih and muhaddith. His commentary on Mashariq al-Anwar, Mabaariq al-Anwar, is printed; also a commentary on al-Manar is printed; and a commentary on Majma al-Bahrayn is a manuscript. His great-grandfather's name was Farishtah. Therefore he is called Ibn Malik in Arabic. 46- Allamah Hasan ibn Ammar al-Shurunbulali (d. 993 AH? d. 1010 AH) is a famous Hanafi faqih of the 11th century. His famous books: (1) Nur al-Idah; (2) Maraqi al-Falah – commentary on Nur al-Idah; (3) Ghunyat Dhawi al-Ahkam fi Bughyat Durar al-Hukkam (printed on the margin of al-Durr); (4) Commentary on Ibn Wahban's Manzumah; (5) al-Tahqiqat al-Qudsiyyah (collection of 48 treatises). Haqaiq al-Manzumah – a commentary on Manzumah al-Khilafiyat by Mufti al-Thaqalayn Allamah Muslimi (25) – the commentator's name is Abu al-Mahamid Mahmud ibn Muhammad al-Ansanji al-Bukhari (d. 227 AH? d. 540 AH?). The manuscript of Haqaiq is in Madinah Munawwarah.
Source pages p. 156

Commentary
This passage is a biographical listing of scholars whose works are central to Hanafi fatwa practice. It begins by introducing Allamah Muhammad Amin 'Amir Badsah', author of a commentary on 'Rasm al-Mufti', then lists several other scholars: Imam Muhammad al-Tahtawi, known for his hashiah on al-Durr al-Mukhtar; al-Bazzazi, author of the famous Fatawa Bazzaziyyah; Qadi Iyad al-Maliki, whose works on hadith and Maliki fiqh are referenced; Ibn Taymiyyah (the Hanbali scholar), included for his fatwa collection and other works; al-Sughdi, a 5th-century Hanafi faqih and author of al-Nutaf al-Hisan; Ibn Malik, an 8th-century Hanafi scholar known for his commentaries; and finally al-Shurunbulali, a leading 11th-century Hanafi jurist whose books Nur al-Idah and Maraqi al-Falah are still taught today. The passage serves to orient the mufti to the authoritative sources and their authors, emphasizing that knowledge of these scholars and their works is foundational for issuing sound fatawa. Notably, Ibn Taymiyyah is a Hanbali, but his fatwa collection is frequently cited across madhhabs.

Key Terms
شرح رسم المفتي (Sharh Rasm al-Mufti): A commentary on the work 'Rasm al-Mufti' by Ibn Abidin, written by Allamah Amir Badsah, which outlines the rules and methodology for issuing fatwas.
فتاوی بزازیہ (Fatawa al-Bazzaziyyah): A collection of fatwas by al-Bazzazi, printed alongside Fatawa Alamgiri, widely used in Hanafi fatwa practice.
نور الایضاح (Nur al-Idah): A concise Hanafi fiqh text by al-Shurunbulali, often studied as a beginner text on worship.
مراقي الفلاح (Maraqi al-Falah): Commentary by al-Shurunbulali on his own Nur al-Idah, widely used as a reference for Hanafi fiqh details.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
Which Hanafi scholar authored 'Nur al-Idah'?
A) Allamah al-Tahtawi
B) Allamah al-Bazzazi
C) Allamah al-Shurunbulali
D) Allamah al-Sughdi

Key Takeaway
The works of al-Shurunbulali, al-Bazzazi, and others are essential references for Hanafi fatwa, and a mufti must know their hierarchy.

Life of the Author
intermediate
7 min
Cross-Madhhab Scholarship: Qadi Iyad and Ibn Taymiyyah in the Hanafi Curriculum
Listing biographies and works of key Hanafi scholars

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to explain why Qadi Iyad (Maliki) and Ibn Taymiyyah (Hanbali) are included in a Hanafi biographical work and state their major works.

Core Idea
A mufti must know authoritative works from other madhhabs to enrich his fatwa research.

The passage includes two non-Hanafi scholars: Qadi Iyad al-Maliki and Ibn Taymiyyah al-Hanbali. Their inclusion reflects the practical reality that a Hanafi mufti often needs to consult works from other schools, especially when the Hanafi sources lack detail or when addressing universal issues like sirah, siyasah, and usul.

Guided Path
1
Identify the two non-Hanafi scholars
Qadi Iyad (Maliki, d. 524 AH) and Ibn Taymiyyah (Hanbali, d. 728 AH).
Qadi Iyad is from the 6th century, Ibn Taymiyyah from the 7th/8th.
2
List their key works as mentioned in the passage
Qadi Iyad: al-Shifa, Tartib al-Madarik, Mashariq al-Anwar, al-Ilma'. Ibn Taymiyyah: al-Sarim al-Maslul, Raf' al-Malam, al-Tawassul, al-Siyasah al-Shar'iyyah, al-Furqan, Fatawa, Minhaj al-Sunnah.
Some works like Fatawa Ibn Taymiyyah are collected volumes.
3
Analyze why these works are included in a Hanafi biographical compilation
These works are widely respected across madhhabs. Al-Shifa is a classic in sirah, Fatawa Ibn Taymiyyah is a major reference for fatwa, and his Minhaj al-Sunnah is key in refuting innovation.
The inclusion does not mean endorsement of their entire fiqh; it means they are valuable resources.
4
Consider the caution for a Hanafi mufti
While consulting these works, a mufti must be aware of the author's madhhab and not automatically adopt their rulings. He should cross-check with Hanafi sources.
Especially for matters where the schools differ.

شرح رسم الملتي
یہ علامہ محمد امین معروف به امیر بادشاہ (متوفی ۹۷۲ھ) کی ہے (۳) المسايره في العقائد المنجية في الآخرة یہ علم کلام کا متن متین ہے۔ مسایرہ کے معنی ہیں ساتھ ساتھ چلنا ۔ چونکہ اس کتاب میں امام غزالی رحمہ اللہ کے رسالہ قدسیہ کی ترتیب ملحوظ رکھی گئی ہے۔ اس لیے مسایرہ نام رکھا ہے۔ علامہ کمال الدین محمد بن محمد معروف بابن ابی شریف قدی شافعی (متوفی ۹۵ھ) نے مسایرہ کی مسامرہ کے نام سے شرح لکھی ہے جو بعض مدارس میں پڑھائی جاتی ہے۔ (۴) زاد الفقیر
مسائل فقہیہ کا مجموعہ ہے ایک سفر میں یہ رسالہ تصنیف فرمایا ہے۔
علامہ قاضی احمد بن محمد طحطاوی ( طهطاوی) رحمہ اللہ (متوفی ۱۲۳۱ھ ) مشہور حنفی فقیه اور علامہ شامی کے استاذ ہیں آپ کی دو کتابیں مطبوعہ ہیں (۱) طحطاوی حاشیہ در مختار چار ضخیم جلدوں میں ہے (۲) طحطاوی حاشیہ مراقی الفلاح آپ کا ایک رسالہ کشف الدین عن بیان المسح
علی الجوربین مخطوطہ ہے۔ صاحب بزازیه علامه کردری ابن البز از محمد بن محمد بن شہاب رحمہ اللہ (متوفی مشہور حنفی فقیہ ہیں۔ علامہ بزازی سے مشہور ہیں آپ کی دو کتابیں مطبوعہ ہیں (۱) الجامع الوجیز جس کا مشہور نام فتاوی بزاز یہ ہے فتاویٰ عالم گیری کے حاشیہ پر از جلد نمبر ۴ تا نمبر ۶ طبع ہوئی ہے ۔ (۲) مناقب کر دری یہ امام اعظم کے مناقب میں دو جلدوں میں ہے مناقب الامام الاعظم اس کا اصل نام ہے۔ قاضی ابو الفضل عیاض بن موسیٰ شخصی رحمہ اللہ ( و ۳۷۶ ه ف ۵۲۴ ) چھٹی صدی کے مشہور مالکی فقیہ اور محدث ہیں۔ آپ کثیر التصانیف ہیں۔ چند معروف کتابیں یہ ہیں (1) الشفاء بتعريف حقوق المصطفی (سیرت نبوی میں بڑی بابرکت کتاب ہے (۲) ترتیب المدارک و تقريب المسالک علمائے مالکیہ کے احوال میں ہے) (۳) مشارق الانوار ( حدیث شریف کی کتاب ہے ) (۴) الالماع الى معرفة اصول الروايه (اصول حدیث میں ہے ) اور غیر مطبوعہ کتابوں میں مسلم شریف کی شرح ہے۔ ۴۳- علامہ ابن تیمیه شیخ الاسلام ابو العباس احمد بن عبد العلیم بن عبد السلام حرانی دمشقی (و فر (۷۲ھ) ساتویں صدی کے جلیل القدر مضبلی فقیہ بڑے محدث کثیر التصانیف عالم اور مجاہد ہیں ۔ آپ کے دادا عبدالسلام بھی بڑے محدث تھے نیل الاوطار کا متن ہمشقی من احادیث
الاحکام ابن تیمیہ جد کی مشہور کتاب ہے اور ابن تیمیہ حفید کی کتابیں یہ ہیں (۱) الصارم المسلول على شاتم الرسول (۲) رفع الملام عن الائمة الاعلام (۳) التوسل والوسيله (۴) السياسة الشرعيه في اصلاح الراعي والرعيه (۵) الفرقان بين اولياء الله واولياء الشيطان (۲) فتاوى ابن تيميه ( ۷ ) منهاج السنة وغيرہ سینکڑوں کتابوں کے مصنف ہیں۔
-۳۴
علامہ سغدی، شیخ الاسلام ابو الحسن علی بن حسین بخاری رحمہ اللہ (متوفی 21 ) پانچویں صدی کے مشہور حنفی فقیہ ہیں۔ آپ کی مشہور کتاب الخف الحسان ہے۔ نتف، نتفة کی جمع ہے جس کے معنی ہیں " تھوڑا سا' کہا جاتا ہے اعطاه نتفة من الطعام: اس نے تھوڑا سا کھانا دیا افادہ نتفة من العلم : اس نے تھوڑا سا علم سکھایا اور حسان حسنہ کی جمع ہے پس الشف الحسان کا ہے: " شاندار باتوں کا مختصر سا مجموعہ" کیونکہ یہ کتاب فتاوی کا انتخاب ہے۔ اس کا زکیا کی ٹوپ کا پی میوزیم میں ہے۔ آپ نے جامع کبیر کی بھی شرح لکھی ہے۔ فتاوی قاضی خان اور فتاوی بزازیہ میں آپ کا کثرت سے تذکرہ آتا ہے آپ شمس الائمہ سرخسی رحمہ
اللہ کے تلمیذ اور بخاری کے قاضی تھے (اعلام ج ۴، ص ۲۷۹ فوائد ببیہ ص ۵۰)
۴۵
ابن ملک علامہ عبد اللطیف بن عبد العزیز رحمہ اللہ (متوفی نے آٹھویں صدی )
کے مشہور حنفی فقیہ اور محدث ہیں آپ کی مشارق الانوار کی شرح مبارق الانوار مطبوعہ ہے نیز المنار کی شرح بھی مطبوعہ ہے اور مجمع البحرین کی شرح مخطوطہ ہے آپ کے پردادا کا نام فرشتہ تھا

His commentary on Mashariq al-Anwar, Mabaariq al-Anwar, is printed; also a commentary on al-Manar is printed; and a commentary on Majma al-Bahrayn is a manuscript. His great-grandfather's name was Farishtah. Therefore he is called Ibn Malik in Arabic. 46- Allamah Hasan ibn Ammar al-Shurunbulali (d. 993 AH? d. 1010 AH) is a famous Hanafi faqih of the 11th century. His famous books: (1) Nur al-Idah; (2) Maraqi al-Falah – commentary on Nur al-Idah; (3) Ghunyat Dhawi al-Ahkam fi Bughyat Durar al-Hukkam (printed on the margin of al-Durr); (4) Commentary on Ibn Wahban's Manzumah; (5) al-Tahqiqat al-Qudsiyyah (collection of 48 treatises). Haqaiq al-Manzumah – a commentary on Manzumah al-Khilafiyat by Mufti al-Thaqalayn Allamah Muslimi (25) – the commentator's name is Abu al-Mahamid Mahmud ibn Muhammad al-Ansanji al-Bukhari (d. 227 AH? d. 540 AH?). The manuscript of Haqaiq is in Madinah Munawwarah.
Source pages p. 156

Commentary
This passage is a biographical listing of scholars whose works are central to Hanafi fatwa practice. It begins by introducing Allamah Muhammad Amin 'Amir Badsah', author of a commentary on 'Rasm al-Mufti', then lists several other scholars: Imam Muhammad al-Tahtawi, known for his hashiah on al-Durr al-Mukhtar; al-Bazzazi, author of the famous Fatawa Bazzaziyyah; Qadi Iyad al-Maliki, whose works on hadith and Maliki fiqh are referenced; Ibn Taymiyyah (the Hanbali scholar), included for his fatwa collection and other works; al-Sughdi, a 5th-century Hanafi faqih and author of al-Nutaf al-Hisan; Ibn Malik, an 8th-century Hanafi scholar known for his commentaries; and finally al-Shurunbulali, a leading 11th-century Hanafi jurist whose books Nur al-Idah and Maraqi al-Falah are still taught today. The passage serves to orient the mufti to the authoritative sources and their authors, emphasizing that knowledge of these scholars and their works is foundational for issuing sound fatawa. Notably, Ibn Taymiyyah is a Hanbali, but his fatwa collection is frequently cited across madhhabs.

Key Terms
قاضي عياض (Qadi Iyad): Abu al-Fadl Iyad ibn Musa al-Yahsubi (d. 524 AH), a Maliki scholar known for his work al-Shifa on the rights of the Prophet.
ابن تيمية (Ibn Taymiyyah): Taqi al-Din Ahmad ibn Abd al-Halim (d. 728 AH), a Hanbali scholar and prolific author whose fatwa collection is widely used across madhhabs.
الشفاء (al-Shifa): A book by Qadi Iyad on the rights and virtues of the Prophet Muhammad, widely studied across madhhabs.
منهاج السنة (Minhaj al-Sunnah): A work by Ibn Taymiyyah refuting Shi'i doctrines, often used in usul and theology.

Key Takeaway
A Hanafi mufti must be familiar with authoritative works from other madhhabs, but must apply them within the framework of the Hanafi school.

Parsing Biographical Entries in Fatwa Methodology
Biographical list of scholars and works

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to identify the key scholars cited in Hanafi fatwa literature and categorize their works by importance for fatwa issuance.

Core Idea
Knowing scholars and their works is the backbone of fatwa authority.

This passage from Rasm al-Mufti lists prominent Hanafi and Shafi'i scholars along with their major works. As a mufti, you must be able to recognize these authorities to properly assess the strength of a cited opinion and to locate the correct source for a given ruling. This lesson will guide you through parsing such biographical entries for practical fatwa methodology.

Guided Path
1
Scan the entry for scholar's name and century
Begin by identifying the scholar's name and approximate period of activity. This helps contextualize their authority and the era of their works.
Pay attention to death dates (متوفی) when given.
2
Note the madhhab attribution
Determine whether the scholar is Hanafi, Shafi'i, or from another school. This is crucial because the reliability of their opinions in Hanafi fatwa varies.
Non-Hanafi scholars like Imam al-Nawawi are included for their hadith strength, not for fiqh authority.
3
Identify the key works listed
Especially note the matns (core texts) and commentaries. Works like Multaqa al-Abhur, Nur al-Idah, and Kitab al-Nawazil are fundamental for fatwa.
Look for phrases like 'مشہور کتاب' (famous book) or 'مطبوعہ' (published).
4
Observe scholarly relationships
Notice teacher-student chains (e.g., al-Sughdi was a student of Shams al-A'imma al-Sarakhsi). This indicates the transmission of knowledge and authority.
Such chains often appear in the text explicitly.
5
Determine relevance to fatwa methodology
Assess whether the work is a primary matn, a commentary, a collection of fatawa, or a hadith reference. This determines how to use it when issuing a fatwa.
Works like Fatawa Qadi Khan and Fatawa al-Bazzaziyyah are direct fatwa references.

-۵۲
قاضی ابو حازم عبدالحمید بن عبدالعزیز سکونی رحمہ اللہ (متوفی ۲۹۲ھ ) تیسری صدی
Start of Rasm al-Mufti. Al-Ahkam is a famous book of Ibn Taymiyya the grandfather, and the books of Ibn Taymiyya the grandson are these: (1) al-Sarim al-Maslul 'ala Shatim al-Rasul, (2) Raf' al-Malam 'an al-A'immah al-A'lam, (3) al-Tawassul wa al-Wasilah, (4) al-Siyasah al-Shar'iyyah fi Islah al-Ra'i wa al-Ra'iyyah, (5) al-Furqan bayna Awliya' Allah wa Awliya' al-Shaytan, (6) Fatawa Ibn Taymiyya, (7) Minhaj al-Sunnah, and others; he is author of hundreds of books. -34. 'Allamah al-Sughdi, Shaykh al-Islam Abu al-Hasan 'Ali ibn Husayn al-Bukhari (d. 21? 5th century) is a famous Hanafi jurist. His famous book is al-Naf' al-Hasan. Nutf is plural of nutfah meaning 'a little'; it is said a'tahu nutfatan min al-ta'am: he gave a little food; afadahu nutfatan min al-'ilm: he taught him a little knowledge; and hasan is plural of hasanah. So al-Naf' al-Hasan means 'a brief collection of splendid statements' because this book is a selection of fatawa. Its manuscript is in the Topkapi Museum. He also wrote a commentary on al-Jami' al-Kabir. He is frequently mentioned in Fatawa Qadi Khan and Fatawa al-Bazzaziyyah. He was a student of Shams al-A'imma al-Sarakhsi and was the qadi of Bukhara (A'lam vol.4 p.279, Fawa'id Bahiyyah p.50). 45. Ibn Malik, 'Allamah 'Abd al-Latif ibn 'Abd al-'Aziz (d. 8th century) is a famous Hanafi jurist and muhaddith. His commentary on Mashariq al-Anwar is Mubariq al-Anwar (published), also a commentary on al-Manar (published), and a commentary on Majma' al-Bahrayn (manuscript). His great-grandfather's name was Farishtah, so in Arabic he is called Ibn Malik. 46. 'Allamah Hasan ibn 'Ammar al-Shurunbulali (993-1069 AH [؟]) is a famous Hanafi jurist of the 11th century. His famous books are: (1) Nur al-Idah, (2) Maraqi al-Falah (commentary on Nur al-Idah), (3) Ghayat Dhawi al-Ahkam fi Bughyat Durar al-Hukkam (printed on the margin of al-Durar), (4) Commentary on the versification of Ibn Wahban, (5) al-Tahqiqat al-Qudsiyyah (collection of 48 treatises of Shurunbulali). Haqa'iq al-Manzumah is a commentary on Manzumah al-Khilafiyyat of Mufti al-Thaqalayn 'Allamah Muslimi; the commentator is Abu al-Mahamid Mahmud ibn Muhammad al-Ansaji al-Bukhari (d. 627? AH). The manuscript of Haqa'iq is in Medina. 48. 'Allamah Ibrahim ibn Muhammad al-Halabi (d. 956 AH) is a famous Hanafi jurist of the 10th century. His famous matn is Multaqa al-Abhur. Other books: (1) Ghunyat al-Mutamalli fi Sharh Munyat al-Musalli (famous as al-Kabiri), (2) al-Saghir (commentary on Munyah), (3) abridgment of al-Qamus, (4) abridgment of Fatawa al-Tatarkhaniyyah, (5) abridgment of al-Jawahir al-Mudiyyah fi Tabaqat al-Hanafiyyah. -49. Imam al-Nawawi, Yahya ibn Sharaf (d. 676 AH) is a famous Shafi'i jurist and great muhaddith of the 7th century. He was born and died in the village of Nawa near Hawran. He has many writings. Among them: (1) al-Minhaj (commentary on Sahih Muslim), (2) al-Taqrib wa al-Taysir (in Usul al-Hadith), (3) Minhaj al-Talibin, (4) Riyad al-Salihin, (5) Tahdhib al-Asma' wa al-Lughat, etc. -50. Tarsusi [Tarsusi?], Qadi al-Qudat 'Allamah Najm al-Din Ibrahim ibn 'Ali al-Baghdadi (d. 758 AH, lived 38 years) is a famous Hanafi jurist and prolific scholar of the 8th century. His book Anfa' al-Wasa'il ila Tahrir al-Masa'il is a fiqh book and is published. It is also known as Fatawa al-Tarsusiyyah. His second book, Wafayat al-A'yan, is manuscript. 51. Faqih Abu al-Layth al-Samarqandi, Imam al-Huda Nasr ibn Muhammad (d. 373 AH) is a famous Hanafi jurist and great figure of the 4th century. His published books: (1) Bustan al-'Arifin, (2) Khizanat al-Fiqh, (3) Tanbih al-Ghafilin, (4) Muqaddimah Abi al-Layth, (5) Kitab al-Nawazil (in this book, issues narrated by Muhammad ibn Shuja' al-Thanji (student of Hasan ibn Ziyad), Muhammad ibn Muqatil al-Razi, Muhammad ibn Salamah al-Bani Nasir ibn Sayti al-Baji, Abu Nasr Muhammad ibn Salam al-Balkhi, Abu Bakr Muhammad ibn Ahmad al-Askaf al-Balkhi (student of Muhammad ibn Salamah), 'Ali ibn Ahmad al-Farisi, Naqib Abu Ja'far Muhammad ibn 'Abd Allah al-Hindwani al-Balkhi (student of Abu Bakr al-Askaf), and Faqih Abu al-Layth himself are collected). Unpublished books: Tafsir al-Qur'an, 'Umdat al-'Aqa'id, Fada'il Ramadan, Sharh al-Jami' al-Saghir, 'Uyun al-Masa'il, Raqa'iq al-Akhbar fi Bayan Ahl al-Jannah wa Ahwal al-Nar, Mukhtalaf al-Riwayah, Shar'ah al-Islam, Usul al-Din, and al-Mabsut, etc. -52. Qadi Abu Hazim 'Abd al-Hamid ibn 'Abd al-'Aziz al-Sukuni (d. 292 AH) [3rd century].
Source pages p. 157

Commentary
This passage is a biographical listing of notable scholars, primarily Hanafi, along with a few others, and their major works. It forms part of the introductory material of a work on the methodology of issuing fatwas (Rasm al-Mufti). The text begins by mentioning Ibn Taymiyya (both grandfather and grandson), then proceeds through numbered entries: al-Sughdi, a 5th-century Hanafi jurist known for his book 'al-Naf' al-Hasan' (a selection of fatawa); Ibn Malik, an 8th-century Hanafi jurist and hadith scholar; al-Shurunbulali, an 11th-century Hanafi jurist famous for 'Nur al-Idah' and 'Maraqi al-Falah'; al-Halabi, the author of the renowned Hanafi matn 'Multaqa al-Abhur'; Imam al-Nawawi, a Shafi'i scholar included for his authority in hadith and fiqh; al-Tarsusi (or Tarsusi), an 8th-century Hanafi jurist whose 'Anfa' al-Wasa'il' is also known as 'Fatawa al-Tarsusiyya'; Abu al-Layth al-Samarqandi, a 4th-century Hanafi jurist and author of 'Kitab al-Nawazil' among many other works; and finally Qadi Abu Hazim al-Sukuni, a 3rd-century scholar. The passage provides details about each scholar's contributions, key books, and sometimes their teachers or students, offering a reference for students of fatwa to understand the authorities cited in Hanafi fiqh works.

Key Terms
ابن تیمیہ (Ibn Taymiyya): Refers to both the grandfather (Majd al-Din, author of al-Ahkam) and the grandson (Taqi al-Din, the famous Hanbali scholar).
ملتقی الا بحر (Multaqa al-Abhur): The famous Hanafi fiqh matn by Ibrahim al-Halabi, widely used in fatwa issuance.
کتاب النوازل (Kitab al-Nawazil): A collection of juridical incidents (nawazil) compiled by Abu al-Layth al-Samarqandi, including earlier authorities.
متن (Matn): A concise core text in Islamic jurisprudence, often memorized and commented upon.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Key Takeaway
A mufti's knowledge of Hanafi scholars and their works ensures correct citation and fatwa reliability.
